4a1(kha): }/ sher ba/ de bas sems ntying pa rtsa bral rgya mtsh nyal/ rigs kyi ba grub btha' thams cad ni gnhi la thlag/ grub btha' lag khyod byung nas rgom pa min/ gni 
4a2(kha): dngos med la grub mtha' bya ba'i ming yang med// dngos med gsal stong e ma he/ rig sbyor blo 'dod tshig gi rang mgo bskor/ ben par bshad bshad kyang tshig rang gi rgyud las ma sbyar la/ 
4a3(kha): bar de'i sgra chen yong dus gang 'dra byed/ sna tshigs snang ba gang shar de/ mkha' la 'jig 'bral med pa nam mkha'i mkhar de ma zin na/ dg sbyor tshig la mkhas kyang thos pa mang

4a5(kha): pa'i mkhar de zungs shig/ rigs kyi bu/ phugs bon nyid kyi rangs rkyang dad gcig dril gyis 'chi khar phan pa de ka rang / de bas dge sbyor tshig dang smra ba mkhas pa ni/ 'thab rtsod bar 
4a6(kha): gyigs zhug spyi ma rtsal/ tsha ba la ser bu'i grang ba tsam/ chu bo re re la gu gzings kyi brgal ba tsam/ de bas sangs rgyas par zhin tu dka'o// gdam ngag gdam pa'i bla ma yang / 
4b1(kha): la la ni rang rig rang la shar nas sangs rgyas pa yang yod/ la la ni ngan song du mun nag nang du / mda' 'phang ba bzhin du song ba yod/ kye ma kyi ma rigs kyi bu de bas phugs/ bon / 
4b2(kha): nyid kyi na la gtod// tbon nyid 'khor badeng sdug skye med klring / klong chen myed pa la skye ba byer mi len/ de bas klong chen spyod pa gal cho'// klong chen ltha ba skyi med a ma 
4b3(kha): ho/ 'jig med lta ba e ma ho/ tshig dang don du 'dres pa'i skyes bu zhig dgos/ sems dang ldan pa ma bu de 'dres pa'i sgom pa zhig dgos/ spyod tshul yug gcig tu 'dres pa 
4b4(kha): dgos/ rang sems stong pa sangs rgyas rang la rnyed pa'i yid chos dgos/ tshig zung don dril rgyud la sbyor ba e ma ho/ snang ba rgya yan gyi spyod pa rtsa bral so so'i lta ba 'dzin med rang 
4b5(kha): gsal gyi lta ba/ bcos med kyi rig pa rang sar zhig/ 'byu bsdran pa rang par glod la rtsar kyi bzung la khrom gyi drel/ lhod kyis zhig la ci rad ltos/ ces lta ba 'dzin med rang 
4b6(kha): gsal gyi lta ba/ ci byung had kyi chod la tsam gyis zhig/ yer gyis zhog la zhig zhig cing / sangs rgyas log na mi 'dug bsam pa de kha 'bras bu yin/ bya byed sna tshogs de la 
5a1(kha): gril gyis thing la/ gnas lugs steng du zhig/ gnyis med kyi snang ba dang byar med dg sbyir 'bras med rgya yan du thing dang / thib med kyi 'bras ba rang chas su shar ba yin/ 
5a2(kha): rang ng rang gi zhes pa de la ngo sprod/ sangs rgyas rang la 'dug pa'i snang sems gcig tu 'dres dgos/ ngng gis ngang la 'dres pa de rtsal sbyang / lha ba thog bab su thong nang gi snyams byed chod/ 
5a3(kha): bar gyi 'dzin pa chod/ rig pa rkyang dad kyi dran pa'i thag pa chod dgos/ yul zhes gcig tu 'dres dgos/ 'gyur med klong du zhi dgos/ 'gyur med klong du zhi nas 'bras bu yin/ rang 
5a4(kha): sa zin pa'i lta ba la/ thabs su shar ba lta ba/ don du gyur pa'i spyod pa/ klong du them pa'i 'bras bu/ sang len thams cad rgyan du shar na bzangngan ci la byed/ gang har nges zin 
5a5(kha): gnyen po bstan mi dgos/ nges shes nang nas shar nango sprod mi dgos/ sku gsum nang nas shar na sangs rgyas su la r/ thams cad rgyan du khyer la lta bas na/ sna tshigs gcig tu 
5a6(kha): sdus la gzhi thog hril le dril/ rig pa rang gsal glod la 'bras bu blo yi rtsol ba zad nas nyams len yin/ ci byas don dang 'gro ba'i sems bskyed brtsi bas bzung / thams 
5b1(kha): cad grogs su 'char ba'i 'gal ba lam du khyer/ gtan du 'grogs kyang sus kyang ma mthong / da ni ngo shes rgyun du gsal ba/ lhtas na ma grub pa 'di sus kyang thas pa ni mi 'dug 
5b2(kha): dgos dus na sleb/ bzung na zin re nad 'gag/ sgom na ma 'ching ba/ sgyur na 'khor ba/ glod na 'char ba/ sangs rgyas lta ba'i sems nyid/ ngo bo snang sred cig dril lta ba rtsa bral 
5b3(kha): rjen pa/ 'bras bu thob med rang chas/ gdam ngag blo 'das rtsa bral/ sgom pa logs su med kyis/ rig pa rangs bzungs/ rang rig rang gi glod la/ ci byed kho rang yin gyi/ sangs 
5b4(kha): rgyas logs na med/ mdo ru sdus na ngo bo gcig/ byin rlabs zhugs las 'byung / rtogs pa rting nas skyes na/ 'khor ba la zhen pa log/ 'khor 'das bon rnams ma bcos thig 
5b5(kha): le gcig la bzhag/ con rnams ngo bo dmigs med cig le gcig la bzhag pa e ma he/ ngo bo car yang dmigs med ste/ ma bcos pa 'di ni mnyam pa'i ye zhes yin/ 
5b6(kha): mnyam med don la kun yang 'dus/ sems dang nam mkha' dbyer med lta bu la/ mtshan nyid gnyis med nam mkha'i rang bzhin can/ ye shes lnga yang sems nyid nam mkha'i rang 
6a1(kha): y/ bzhin gnas/ cer yang rtsal med hun gyis grub/ gnyis du med pa gsung du bon lemao/ rang 'byung ma bcos mnyam pa'i ye shes yin/ rtsol ba med par / 
6a2(kha): hun gyis grub/ bla na med par yang dag 'bras bya'o// stong pa mi long bya ba zhan tan don rnams kun/ yo zhes chen po'i na la dgongs shing phyi khyab nam mkha' 'dra/ ye nas stong 
6a3(kha): zhing bdag med ye shes te/ mya ngan 'das dang stong nyid ye shes gnyis su med do// bon rnams gsal la sgrib med zang thal yin/ gsal stong gnyis med e ma ho/ gang gi rid 'beb 
6a4(kha): la 'di ltar bya/ snam bu 'phrad du mtho bdun gyen la mtho d/ de la sgom thag bya/ mtshan la skad nas rkad r lag pa bril le dril/ nyin la sked pa gtsun/ sgom thag khug 
6a5(kha): len gnyis byed/ tkhug len gnyis la 'bring ba bskyag la sked pa gtun/ drod peb gong ltar bya/ nyin mtshan la mi gzhan gyi mi mthong ba de ltar bya/ dang po ga lag mang po'i rgyud 
6a6(kha): then par bya/ de nas zhag po re re la lce bra ba la ba dang / zla ba gcig nas ras rkyang bya/ rlung bzung gong ltar gtun pa gal che/ rtsa rlung drid 'bebs ag tham/ gsal la stong zhing 
6b1(kha): bdag med la/ dngos po mtshan ma gsal ba ma yin/ gsal stong gnyis med nam mkha'i rang bzhin las/ mnyam nyid don la s+dzogs pa'i bcos su med/ 'gyur med klong du yi 
6b2(kha): shes yongs su s+dzogs/ lha ba snang stong skye 'gag rtag chad sang len med/ bdag dang 'khor 'das rang bzhin bdag nyid mnyam pa chen por s+dzogs/ nga dang rang bzhin bdag nyid dbyings kyi 
6b3(kha): kling / lta ba phyi nang med pa gdal khyab mnyam pa chen po'o// lta ba la mtshon du med cing bon rnams thams cad mnyam pa nyid du 'dus/ ltha ba mthar thug gi le'u ste gnyis pa'o// 
6b4(kha): kun tu bzang po mtha' dbus med pa'i klong la phyag 'tshal lo// yi dam stag la me 'bar gyis/ su gri dkar po lta ba'i sdzong chen la gsum ste/ de bsgom pa ni 'khor 'das yi 
6b5(kha): stong mnyam nyid la/ sgom pa'i rgyu ni dbyings las 'bras bu/ rgyu 'bras gnyis su med pa'i e ma ho/ 'bras bu rgyu la rgyu yang 'bras bu chen po gnyis su med do// so sor tha me dad 
6b6(kha): do// 'bras bu phye ba dkar nag gi rkun ma gda'/ brtson 'grus rta po yang yang rgyug/ nga rang bzhin bdag nyid chen po lhun gyis grub/ gol ba'i na 'khor 'das bon rnams 
7a1(kha): bcos shing bslad du med/ 'di rgya che togs dka' ba'i thun mongs ma yin no// de ci yi pbyer zhe na/ khyab ni kun chen po yin te/ ye shes la rang gis rang la nyon / 
7a2(kha): mongs pa 'ong pa'i san nang du bsdums pa dang 'dra bs ma mthongs// gdam ngag bstan pa'i bla ma la ma thug sangs rgyas mi 'byung / rigs kyi bu/ sgom pa 'khor 'das bon rnams sgom 
7a3(kha): pa dka' ste/ nam mkha' rgya mtsho kha gting med/ khyung dang nyas kyang bcad pa dka' ba bzhin/ sgom pa bon rnams nam mkha' 'dra la spro bsdu med/ con rnams gting dpag 
7a4(kha): brtag dka' sems kyi rang bzhin/ gnhen rab sgam ste mdzad pa med/ sems can sbrin te bcos su med/ sgom pa'i thog ma nas spros pa'i mtshan ma thams cad bral lo//

7b1(kha): pa'o// sgom pa 'khrul rtog byung na/ mi 'khrul mi rtog dmigs su mchis sam zhus/ sgom ni mi dmigs pa la 'khrul rtog g.yo ba'i zhes pa rdul tsam yang med do// lha'i /

10a1(kha): le' ste gsum pa'o// kun du bzang po mtha' dbus med pa'i klong la pbyag 'tshal lo// yiM dam stag la mi 'bar gyis/ snga gri dkar po lta ba'i rdzong / dpyod pa ni

12a5(kha): yin skye med a ma ho/ mi 'ong ma 'gro mnyam nyid don rtogs spres bral chen po'// spyod pas ngo bo spyod pa gnyis med dbyer med so so tha ma dad d// spyod pa 'khor 'das bon la 
12a6(kha): dbye ba med/ 'khor 'das bon rnams sgyu ma lta bu la/ ceir yang ma yin dngos po stong / gzugs brnyan cghu zla gzha' tshen lta bu 'ra/ bon la skye 'gag med pa stong pa yin/ 
12b1(kha): / spyod pas 'khor 'das bon la g.yo ba med/ g.yo ba med pas phyi nang steng 'og med/ rgyu 'bras bdag gzhan dmigs med gsal stong mdun rgyab phyi nang med/ rigs kyi bu rgyal po / 
12b2(kha): chen po gcig la/ mkhar sgo moa mang po yod pa zhig gda'/ rgyal po la blon po sum brgya drug bu yo// rtogs pa'i dus nas ye shes sum brgya drug cu yin/ ma rtogs dus na 
12b3(kha): nyon mongs pa brgyad khri bzhi stong rgyas pa yin/ rgyal pos 'khor gyi sgo mo gnyis nas gzigs pas/ phyi yang stong pa nang yang stong pa/ gsal ba la dngos 'dzin mi 'dug/ phye dang 
12b4(kha): nang med gzhal yas khang / mkhar ni lus po yin/ rgyal po ni sems yin/ sgo mo mang po na bu ga sgo dgu yin/ blon po dran rig sna tshogs mi dran dgu dran 'di yin/ sgo / 
12b5(kha): ni mig gnyis yin/ mig nas gzigs pas phyi nang gnyis med gsal ba stong / gsal stong gnyis med a ma he/ spyod pas 'khor ba mya ngan 'das pa dmigs med pa/ ngdang 
12b6(kha): bdag tu 'dzin pa ga la srid/ kun kyang byang chub sems su gcig/ byang chub bdag med stong pa/ 'khor 'das sems la rang bzhin med/ kun gsal rang bzhin med/ mnyam nyid 
13a1(kha): @/ chen po la/ yar la mi re mar la mi tog/ 'gyur ba med pa nam mkha' lta bu'i rang bzhin las/ re ba dogs pa ga la yod/ spyod pa nyon mongs bdud bzhi zeal 
13a2(kha): gyis gnon/ zil gyis bzhon pas ye shes chen po yin/ spyod pas dbyings chen mi 'gyur le'u ste bzhi pa'o// / kun tu bzang po mtha' dbus med pa'i klong la phyag 'tshal / 
13a3(kha): lo// yi dam stag la me 'bar gyis/ su gri dkar po lta ba'i s+dzong / de nas byang chub sems bstan pa la gnyis te/ gzhi 'khor ba 'khor med gnyis su med pa'i ye shes nyid du 
13a4(kha): gsal/ g.yo mad spros bral mtha' la 'das pa mnyam pa nyid do// nam mkha' snang srid gsal zhing ma khyab med/ mkha' la sprin tshogs dgos pa med pa nam mkha'i ang du ni/ 
13a5(kha): ban rnams mkhyen pa'i ye shes nyid du gsal/ gzhi rnam par dag pa la 'dzin pa med/ bcon rnams mnyam pa nyid la zla/ yod med spros mthar ye shes s+dzogs na ci yang mkhyen/ 
13a6(kha): bon rnams ye nas ma bsgrib gnyis su med/ 'gyur ba sna tshogs gang 'byung yang mnyam pa nyid kyi don la s+dzogs/ gzhi la don mthun smra bas sangs rgyas yin/ dug lnga'i gnyen 
13b1(kha): po ye zhes snyom par bya/ gzhi gzhal yas khang du/ 'khrul snang sna tshigs shig shig btang / dug dang nyon mongs la ye shes ci 'dra ba/ rgyu 'bras don dam dmigs med ngn du thim/ 
13b2(kha): gzhi la spyod pa'i sems ni sangs rgyas yin/ con rnams ngo bo dngos med/ des na spros bral mtha' 'das yin/ don ni ma bcos dbyings su sangs rgyas te/ gzhi ni mi 'gyur g.sung 
13b3(kha): dug dmigs med dngos med yin/ mi 'gyur gsung drung nam mkha' bzhin du gnas/ 'gyur ba med pa bon nyid dbyings la bcos su med/ ye nas yod pa 'khor 'das gzhi la bcos 
13b4(kha): su med/ 'gyur med ngo bo ma bcos dngos med gan la bzhags/ bon nyid rang bzhin nam mkha' lta bu la/ gzhi la rtogs pa med pa yi bdal chen po yin/ gdal pa chen po ya 
13b5(kha): nas sangs rgyas la/ 'gyur med dbyings nyid sems kyi rang bzhin yin/ ye nas sangs rgyas ye shes 'bras bu thobs/ sems kyi rang bzhin bcon rnams kun/ ye shes chen po thob 
13b6(kha): pa bdal pa chen po'i sangs rgyas/ sems kyi rang bzhin zad pa med/ 'gyur med ye shes yi sangs rgyas/ gzhi nas kha gting med pa ye nas yod/ dg med dbyings nyid ye nas 
14a1(kha): sems kyirng bzhin me/ sems kyirg bzhin yi shes yai sangs rgyas pa'i phyir/ 'khor 'das bon rnams dpag med yai sangs rgyas/ sems kyirng bzhin gsal stong / 
14a2(kha): gnyis med zhes na 'bras ba yin/ gzhi nas rgya ma chad pa ye yod yin/ 'gyur ba dngos med rnam rtog 'phro rgod d// mu med klong du tham la ye sangs rgyas/ sems kyi rang bzhin 
14a3(kha): mu med 'byams yas mtha' 'das chen po yin/ sems kyi rang bzhin 'bras bu thob pa yin/ kye rigs kyi bu/ rtsib khung na me btang nas me zhe nas rtsib kzhung gdud pa chad pa 
14a4(kha): bzhin/ stong gsal 'dzin med du sgom pa yin/ kye rigs kyi bu/ sems rang bzhin 'byams yas klong du yi sangs rgyas/ 'khor dang mya ngan 'das pa'i bon rnams kun/ bla med 
14a5(kha): g.sung drung dbyings su mu med dbyings nyid ya sangs rgyas/ gzhi med 'gyur med yi sangs rgyas/ nyon mongs sems can 'khrul pa'i blo la ma yengs zhig/ 'khrul pa ngan song 'khor bar 
14a6(kha): 'gro/ bden don spyod par 'gyur med yai sangs rgyas/ rtogs nas mu med bcon du ya sangs rgyas/ ma rtogs rgyu drug khams gsum 'khor zhing ltung / de'i 'khrul pa'i blo bag shig gi 
14b1(kha): btang / yi sangs rgyas pa'i don la kha gting med/ gdal ba chen po dpag med rtogs med nam mkha'i rang bzhin can/ dper nam mkha'i 'byung ba kun shing yin/ sems dang 
14b2(kha): sems las byung ba'i ting 'dzin 'phel 'grib med/ rig pa snang stong mtha' las mi spyod spros dang bral/ 'khor 'das bon dang gnyis med nam mkha'i dbyings su bla dang 'dra/ de yangs 
14b3(kha): rdore brag rtsi shing ma yin te/ 'du 'bral ye nas med pa'i rtsa bral chen po yin/ gzhi rtsa bral ye nas bcos su med/ lus kyi rig pa mdangs 'char ba ni/ nang nas 'char ba 
14b4(kha): phyi nang med pa yin/ dper na nam mkha'i nye ma dang 'dra/ lus dang rig pa yang de dang 'dra/ dngos med gsal ba a ma haM/ ma bcos nga la gsal ba rang rig ye shes yin/ ngo bo med 
14b5(kha): pa gsal ba bon nyid kling / ngo bo 'byung ba s+dzogs chen don la 'gal/ mu med gsal ba spyod pa lhun grub sku/ gzhi rtsa med pa mthar la thug pa ye nas med/ s+dzogs chen ngo bo 
14b6(kha): gzhi stong rtsa bral la/ 'jig pa'i bya ba ye nas med/ ngo bo 'byung gnas 'jig pa yin/ dngos med gsal stong 'jig med gzhal yas khang / 'jig tshad gzhal yas khang la / 
15a1(kha): 'dg/ 'bral ba med par gzung du gsol/ ngag gi smra brjod gsal sting 'dzin du bzhag/ rigs kyi bu snang srid khyab bdal yon tan ma 'gag pa/ mthar tchod dangos 
15a2(kha): med nam mkha' lta bu ste/ rig pa ye shes mnyam nyid spros bral gsal la 'dzin pa med/ stong la dngos po med/ sgom med skye med gnyis su med/ sang len med pa lhag mthong 
15a3(kha): kha dog dngos med yi ge med/ g.yo ba med pa bon rnams nam mkha' lta bu de/ ying med gsal ba rang bzhin yin/ stong pa'i rang bzhin bdag nyid can/ gzhi ni ye shes stong pa'i 
15a4(kha): rang bzhin yin/ rang bzhin ma g.yis mnyam pa nyid/ mi ma yin gyis cho 'phrul ci byung yang / log nas ma 'byung rang gi sems la 'byung / sems kyi snang ba gang byung yang / 
15a5(kha): gzhi yi steng du bril le dril/ 'di ni sems nyid yong s+dzogs theg pa chen po yin/ gzhi la dngos po med pa rig pa'i ye shes so// gzhi la dngos med 'byams yas rgya chad mtha' / 
15a6(kha): gtad med pa dang / rig pa shar bnam mkha' rang bzhin can/ rig pa'i ye shes so s ma yin no// 'khor 'das rang bzhin dag tu med/ gzhi ni dmigs med nam mkha' 'dra/ 
15b1(kha): gzhi rtsa med pa stong pa'i rang bzhin can/ can rnams stong pa'i rang bzhin nam mkha' 'dra/ bla med yongs s+dzogs dmigs med dgongs pa nam mkha' 'dra/ rig pa gsal la mi 
15b2(kha): g.yo mtha' dang bral/ cbon rnams stong pa'i rang bzhin/ tshig dang sgra brjod mkhas pa shes la don med yin/ smra brjod mkhas na zhe sdang che/ zhe sdang nyon mongs sugs shing yin/ 
15b3(kha): theg pa 'og ma tshig dang smra brjod brten/ tshig gi lung bstan ku 'debs 'dra/ de nyid mtshan nyid pa'i lugs so// yang gsang gdam pa stong pa ni/ dang po theg pa chen po ye klong du ma 
15b4(kha): gyur the/ glong du gyur nas tshig don gnyis ka bsre/ tshig gi don khrid yangs med bzhags/ gsang sngags zab mo sems kyi 'tsho skyongs yin/ ya cha ma bral gnyis med gcig tu 
15b5(kha): dril/ de ltar byas na nags kyi re la me lce 'dra/ ces ston pas gsungs so// sems rtsi gcig tu dril la yings med skyongs/ gzhi ni dmigs med chen po nam mkha'i tshul/ 
15b6(kha): ting 'dzin zab mo 'di la spyod pas/ mun khang sgrin me btegs pa 'dra/ shes rab chen po'i dmigs med klong du spyod/ bsod nams 'bras bu stong nyid ma bu 'phrad nas bde/ yi klong 
16a1(kha): // 'gyur med byang sems gnyis med bzhag par bya/ rgyu las 'byung ba gzhi med rtsa bral steng du bzhag/ gzhi la 'khrul pa ye nas med/ lam nas gzhi tshig ma 
16a2(kha): bslab bar/ de 'khrul nas khams gsum du kha 'khor rgyu drug tu lus blang / gzhi la zen na rangs zin pa yin/ rang s zin pas brtson 'grus rta po yang yang rgyug/ rgyug pa'i / 
16a3(kha): chab brel chu la them pa ltar/ nam mkha' phrin dang khu brlungs zhi ba ltar/ dri le lhod de 'bo la bnag/ de ltar bnag pa s+dzogs pa chen po e ma te/ gzhi la 'khrul pa med 
16a4(kha): pa'i e ma ngo mtshar che'o// gzhi byang chub sems su bstan pa'i le'u ste lnga pa'o// / tsi// / kun tu bzang po mtha' dbus med pa'i klong la phyag 'tshal lo// ston pa stag la me 
16a5(kha): 'bar gyis/ su gri dkar po lta ba'i s+dzong / da lam gzhi tshog pab pa ye zshes sgron me la gsum ste/ lam gsal ba mkha' la nyi ma lhar yod/ lam la nyam ng med pa khyung dang 
16a6(kha): seng ge' bu ltar nyamsg med/ dpa' rtsal can bas tig gdug med/ rig pa gsal ba'i rang la 'char/ gang zhig rig pa shar bas gsal ba yin/ rang dbang rang gi thob nas rab 
16b1(kha): mchog rgyal ba yin/ mtshan bcas dbang thob dang ma thob phan gnod mi 'dug/ rang dbang rang gi thob nas kun thobs rgyal po yin/ skyo ngas med pas rig pa rang shar kun snyoms 
16b2(kha): sems/ lam la g.yo rtsol med pas 'dzin chags med/ gang zhig shes rab can gyi snying rje bdag phyogs med/ lam la 'khrul pa'i dgra gnyen yod pas brtson 'grus bya/ 
16b3(kha): bsam don ting 'dzin bsgoms pas re dgs med/ thabs la mkhas pa'i shes rab rtsal gyis sbyangs/ kun 'byungngan song sgo khegs gnon rgyal po yin/ byung yang sems nyid nga 
16b4(kha): nas byung / theim yang sems nyid ngang la thim/ blo rtsal sbyang la nyam nga med pa khrol dgos/ byung csher bzod pa med na btang snyoms med/ 'gyur ldog bsam don med na ltung ba med/ 
16b5(kha): 'khor ba chags pa med na 'khrul pa med/ nyon mongs med na ro dgs med/ 'khrul pa med na shes rab med/ ltung ba med na nyon mongs med/ re dgs med na 'khor chags med/ de 
16b6(kha): lhar yin kyang ngo bo gcig/ 'khor ba'i mtshan ma yod med nam mkha'i ngigs dang 'dra/ zag med mtshan ma ci ltar yang na nam langs nyi shar 'dra/ nam mkha'i nyi zer dbyer med 
17a1(kha): ltar/ nam mkha'i gs 'dra snang ba sna tshigs shig shig btang / rang bzhin med pa zhes na shes rab yin/ shes rab phung po nam mkha' 'dra/ phyi ya yul rnams tong 
17a2(kha): nyid phyi stong yin/ phyi nang gnyis stong 'dzin med 'dus byas 'dus ma byas/ rang bzhin mtshan ma med/ phyi nang yul rnams stong zad yin/ stong pa'i nang du gsal ba yin/ gsal 
17a3(kha): la dngos 'dzin med pa yin/ stong nyid de la ye shes rang 'byung rang shar yin/ lam nas stong nyid ang du stong pa ye shes stong / stong pa nyid kyang ye shes nam mkha' 'dra/ rang bzhin med 
17a4(kha): pas rang gi mtshan nyid yin/ nang 'dzin yid dang ngo bo yid dang stong 'dzin bon/ ngng snyoms stong zad gsal ba ye shes 'di gsal yin/ nam mkha' kun 'byung ye shes phung po des ni 
17a5(kha): ma khyab med/ ye shes phung po gzhi rtsa mthar la thug pa med/ lam nas gdong zhing skye 'gag med// skye 'gag med pas stong nyid ma bu mdzal/ de la ye nas kha dang gting med/

17b1(kha): dran sting / re ma ra stong / dri zham stong / rna ba tshar stong / mig mthong stong / lus reg bya 'jam pa yang / skyed pa sdhug pa dga' ba mi dga' ba yid pa med pa kun stoing ba kun 
17b2(kha): gnsgal la 'dzin med stong pa yin/ dran la stong pa nyid du rtogs pa'i gal khyab chen po yin/ lus sems tshor ba'i bon ni stong pa yin/ lam la mi 'khrul gni tsig cag

18a1(kha): / byb/ song 'khyams/ can rnams dmigs med snyoms la ma bcos ngang la bzhag/ rig pa'i ye shes rang la shar ba'i ngo bo med la/ dngos med stong / can rnams stong pa nyid du

2a3(cha'o): gtogs pa las kyi 'brel pa'i ma dang sring mo rnams/ a khrag zan du btsug cing dam sdzas dmar la brten/ da ni lus kyi dgra bgegs dag la thad mi 'tshal/ rtogs 
2a4(cha'o): pas bdag bsgral/ grub pas gnan bsgral nas/ dus gsum gzhin rab bstan pa bsung bar bya'o// cesso// / ston pas bka' stsal pa/ e mango mtshar che/ 
2a5(cha'o): da ni ye zhes lha'i snying po dang du long zhes gsungs so// de nas bla ma chen po la zhus/ stag la me 'bar gyis 'di skad ces gsungs so// sna la dbang dang sngags kyi lung 
2b1(cha'o): stsal/ de nas bsnyen sgrub ba thu rtsal sgrubs/ de nas tshe sgrub/ da lha ma sgrub na bdag po med pa'i nor dang 'dra/ de nas dang po lta ba bsgrub pa ni/ can ye nas spros dang bral// 
2b2(cha'o): mtshan ma'i rtog rtul yang med/ cer yang dngos po stang / ngo bo ma grub rang bzhin stong / stong pa'i ng la gang gnas pa/ ma bcos ye nas gnas pa stag las ya sku/ 'di la basdng
2b3(cha'o): cing gcad du med/ bshig tu bsung bya gang gi yang / 'di bas lhag ni rnyed pa dka'/ de phyir lta ba 'di nyid tag tu dran par bya/ stong nyid sa la rang 'byung sku/ rang nyid khro chen stag la'i 
2b4(cha'o): sku/ sna tshogs 'char ba gang 'byung yang / mi dmigs stong pa'i sna la bzhag/ rgyal ba gnhen rab kyis bka' stsal pa/ lta ba byang chub sems la 'gyur ba med/ 'gyur ba med 
2b5(cha'o): pa gsung drung thob pa ni/ kun bzang yin te/ nam mkha'i rigs la 'gyur ba med ces gsungs so// sems rang 'byung gi gnen lha 'di dkar po sems spros bral nam mkha' 'dra 
2b6(cha'o): ba/ lha'i skyabs su med/ 'dre yi za ru med/ ces pas/ cho 'drul sna tshogs 'char ba/ mi skye mi 'gag nam mkha'i rang bzhin can/ rang 'byung ye shes thig le'i klong na 
3a1(cha'o): srdzogs/ deyang skye bdpon gyi sku/ ton nyid thugs rje mnyam snyom can/ sdu 'brul thabs kyi yings la kbyag/ 'di zer ba mi 'thad na/ nyon ming sems can / 
3a2(cha'o): 'khrul pa'i skye she 'byung / zhes gsungs pa'o// kun bzang dang sems can ni/ gzhi ni gcig pa la/ gzhi n ma bcos ye nas lhuan gyis grub/ kun bzang rtogs pa'i s+dzogs 
3a3(cha'o): sangs rgyas/ gzhi la 'khrul pa med de/ sems can lam nas 'khrul pa'i 'khor bar 'khyams/ sems nyid mnyam par bzhag pa ni/ rgya mtso blung gi ma bskyed pa/ nam 
3a4(cha'o): mkha' la nyi ma dang zer lhar/ rgya mtsho' gtiang du zer yod pa ltar/ mar me s blung gis ma bskyed pa/ bon nyid kyi dbyings su sems nyid thig le bzhag/ ces gsungs so// sems ni / 
3a5(cha'o): nam mkha' dangs pa 'dra ba la/ gsal ba ye zhes ma 'gag pa/ nyid la nyid bzhag pa'o// zhe sdang dang / 'dod chags/ gti mug/ phrag dog dang / nga rgyal 'khrul pa'i/ nyon 
3a6(cha'o): mongs bdud 'dra ba la/ byams pa'i sems bskyed/ brtson 'grus byas la/ ye shes sems ni ci 'dra gtong / bon nyid ma bcos pa de bzhin du / sems nyid de yang de bzhin du 
3b1(cha'o): gnas pa'o// con nyid nam mkha' ye dag la/ sems nyid gsal ba 'd byung nas/ mkha' klong ye nas rnod yangs la/ mi dmigs ng la bzhag go ces so// thig le mznor ba / 
3b2(cha'o): gsal gdab la/ yongs su khyab pa la/ sems kyi tshad ni zen pa med/ skye ne dang 'du 'bral med pa'i don rang la yod/ sems nyid rang snang la shar ba'o// ye nas yod pa'i don ma 
3b3(cha'o): bcos pa/ yod med gnyis kyi mtha' las 'das pa'o// sems la dngos po mtshan ma med/ 'dus byas thig le nyag gcig go/ lta ba'i zhes stong gnyis med mnyam pa la/ gnyis 
3b4(cha'o): med sems so ser ma yin/ lha ba skye med sems ni gnyis med khod snyoms la bril le gzigs/ cho 'dul dran rig gang byung yang / ye stong gnyis med mnyam par bzhag/ lha 
3b5(cha'o): ba bon nyid rgya mtsho'i klong du / rin chen gser gyi 'gyur ba nya mo de/ nya mo 'phyo ba'i rgya mtsho snags/ rgya mtsher bon nyid klong du nya mo gnyis med nyal nas theg pa chen po'o// 
3b6(cha'o): g/ con nyid dbyings nas bcud 'byung la/ nye zer tshul dang chu zla bzhin du/ thams cad nam mkha'i dbyings su rang bzhin yai sangs rgyas/ gzugs med khyab bdal nam mkha' 
4a1(cha'o): bar snang la/ dngos med yul nas gzugs med sku gnas pa/ rtogs pa med pa rang bzhin ye nas gnas pa la/ mkha' dang klong du zad pa med pa/ khyung chen gnam / 
4a2(cha'o): 'phang gcod pa shes/ sems nyid kyang de bzhin du gsal/ ye yod bon la y khyab 'gags med sems bzhag/ kun bzang s la yi yod kun gnas te/ 'khrul pa blo'i bdag dang 
4a3(cha'o): gzhan du bzung / bdag dang gzhan du mi bzung 'gyur med bdag/ bag chags de la zhen bab zo chu'i rgyud ma 'dra/ zo chu'i rgyud ma bcad pas/ kun bzang s la ye shes rang dbang 
4a4(cha'o): thob pas/ lha ba nam mkha'i dbyings ni 'phyo/ dbyings chen mtha' dang bral bas/ gnod pa'i dgra rnams ye nas med/ zad pa med par rgyal po bde ba'i mchog/ kun rtogs rig 
4a5(cha'o): pa dmar thag bcad pas/ nyi zer ma la 'dus pa bzhin du gcig la 'dus/ thugs rje nam mkha' ye shes dbyings su rol/ bon nyid cig le ye nas khyab bdal du gnas pa/ 
4a6(cha'o): sems nyid yang de ltar du gnas/ thugs ni ye shes nam mkha' bcos su med/ sems zer ba'i rig pa 'di/ ye shes kun la mnyam pa/ khams gsum khyab bdal du gnas pa'i 
4b1(cha'o): sa 'di la/ dngos po mtshan ma med pa la grub/ gsal ba'i 'od zer phyogs bcur khyab pa'i gnyis med du s+dzogs pa/ stong zhing bdag med pa kun khyab chen po'o// rang rig pa'i yi 
4b2(cha'o): shes ye nas mtha' thams cad las 'das pa yi nas khyab chen po ni// bon 'di lan gsum thob nas/ ma rtogs kyang ngan song du mi 'gro ba ni/ ston pang yi kha'i len/ lta ba 
4b3(cha'o): 'di ni bon nyid dbyings togs pa chen po'// bon nyid sems ni ma bcoMs par bzhag/ stong dang mi stong gnyis ka dbyings nyid pa la 'das/ snang srid thams cad 'byung yang nam mkha' 
4b4(cha'o): ngang nas 'byung / gnas kyang nam mkha'i ngang la gnas/ thim yang nam mkha'i ngang la thim/ nam mkha' la thog ma tha ma med pas nub rgyu med/ bon nyid sems nyid nam 
4b5(cha'o): mkha'i dbyings su gcig ces gsungs so// bon gyi sgo mo brgyad khri bzhi stong / 'byung yang bon nyid klong nas 'byung / gnas kyang bon nyid klong nas gnas/ thim yang bon nyid klong na 
4b6(cha'o): thim/ dus gsum du 'gyur ba med pa s+dzogs pa chen po'o// srog dbugs tshad thams cad/ 'byung yang sems las 'byung / gnas kyang sems las gnas/ sangs rgyas sa yang 
5a1(cha'o): sems kyi nga rgyas/ sems bde chen la dus gsum du 'gag pa med pas/ dmigs med du bstan pa'o// zhes gsungs so// sangs rgyas sems can gnyis la/ sems / 
5a2(cha'o): can thams cad la 'chi 'phos yod kyang / sangs rgyas ni byang chub kyi sems 'gyur ba med pa g.sung drung gi sku thob pa yin/ skye 'chi med pa'i phyir/ brtsal du med pa bon nyid 
5a3(cha'o): dbyings nas/ gsal la ma yengs pa bzhags pa ni/ 'bras bu thams cad lhun la s+dzogs pa'i yi khyab chen po'// yang rgyal ba gnhen rab gyis gsungs pa/ nam mkhas gar 
5a4(cha'o): khyab sems kyis khyab pas/ sems khyab pa chen po'i yo zhes can/ kun gn dang rig pa la 'du 'bral med pas/ lta ba ye zhes chen po'// sems kyis nas rig pa'i bcud 
5a5(cha'o): shar ba/ bon nyid klong nas thams cad mtha' las 'das/ gnyis med spros bral chen po'o// khyung chen sgong rgya ral pa dang / seng go'i 'khru rgya ral pa dang / rnal 'byor lus rgya ral 
5a6(cha'o): pa dang gsum/ khyung gi sgong rgya nang nas gzhog dug rgyas nas nam mkha' la lding / seng gi' bu rgya ral nas re brag gang la tsogs pa med/ rnal 'byor lus rgya ral nas mtha' 
5b1(cha'o): bral s+dzogs pa chen po'o// byang chub kyi sems ni skye 'cshi med pas na g.yung / 'du 'bral med pas na dung / gnyis su med pa'i don lus rgya ral/ sems mtshan ma kha dag can / 
5b2(cha'o): du ma yin/ byang chub kyi sems ni mtha' dang dbus med pas/ mtha' bral chen po'o// lta ba mthar thug gting 'dzin bstan pa'o// / de yang sgom ni mtha' bral chen po / 
5b3(cha'o): bsgom/ mtha' bral dngos med mthar thug sems/ zhes gsungs so// phye sgrub bstan 'gro sgrib sbyong du tre su ya sgrub pa dang / nang sgrub su gri nag po'i mdel thung le'u sngags dang 
5b4(cha'o): bcas pa/ gs sgrub su gri dmar po dang / yang gs sgrub pa ye shes ma dpung dang / lta ba su gri dkar po la gsum ste/ sngon du dbang gi sgo dbye ba dang / sngags sems de rnams 
5b5(cha'o): mdzoad dang sgo mo lha mig 'adra/ sngags la sems phyogs gces/ sems phyogs la sngags gcis/ 'dzoms pa gal che zhes gsungs so// sgom legs pa dus da lta rang dbang thob 
5b6(cha'o): pa'i dus sgom/ brtson 'grus bskyed pa'i dus bab/ tshe 'di dang phyi ma bar do gsum la/ dus rgyun du sgom 'chal s rang la ma bsgyur bar/ kyi ma skal ldan rigs kyi bu/ blo thag / 
6a1(cha'o): gdng nas cad kyi tshod/ tshe rabs thog ma med pa nas/ da lta bar du 'khyams/ sems ni 'gyod pa drag po zhig ni yin/ lus rang gi rgyud ma la sbyar na/ tche bye ma 
6a2(cha'o): zer ba kho kha yin/ dpyad zhes na go bzhin rang mgo ma skor cig/ mthar ni 'gyod pa drag po zhig ni 'ong ba skad/ kye ma rigs kyi bu/ yid rting nas ma khrel ba snang ba yeng med du 
6a3(cha'o): 'bol le/ rig pa gdong med du pyed de/ dmigs med du nyed de zhog dang / sgom pa sangs rgyas yang dag yin/ phyogs 'jog gi blo ma bzhag/ snang ba gang shar gyi mkhar de nam 
6a4(cha'o): mkha'i rang bzhin mkha'/ mkhar de la rgyun tu ma bral/ de la bral nas bdud kyi bsru ba phog pa yin/ kye ma yang cig gsen dang rigs kyi bu/ 'gyu ba'i rjes 'grel mshor ba/ 
6a5(cha'o): rig pa klong yang bzhag cig/ mi rtog nang nas mzhr nas/ rtogs pa'i ye shes gana 'ong / rtogs pa'i snang ba gang shar grogs su shes dgos/ sgom mkhan gyi dran thag ma chod 
6a6(cha'o): na/ blos byas sgom pa ni/ 'byung ba'i nang du 'gyu ba'i dus su bon nyid rtogs/ 'byung ba'i phyi las 'gyu ba'i dus su nam mkha'i dmigs su rtogs/ 'dod kyang yi stong rtsa bral sgom/ 
7b1(cha'o): gting na bskyed pa rgyal ba'i bstan pa nam mkha' 'dra bas/ rigs kyi bu/ bla ma'i gdams ngag nyi ma 'dra/ phyogs med kun la snyoms pa la/ gsal sgrib med pa la nyi rang med 
7b2(cha'o): ye nas med par gda'/ sgom cig chen gyi gdams ngag sbrang rtsi 'dra/ sgom mkhan med pa dus da lha ci byed rang dbang thob pa la/ sems ngos bzung gtad pa med pa la/ chags sdang 
7b3(cha'o): bsogs pa ye nas med/ phyi snang ba'i 'char tshul gzha' tchen 'dra/ gzha' tchen dngos med ye stong chen po la/ de yang gsal ba la rang bzhin med pa la/ yid 'gyu ba la dran pa 
7b4(cha'o): ser bu 'dra/ 'dzin med pa shig shig btang / 'di yang skal ldan rgyud la sbyangs/ nga bdag gi che ba khrol zhig/ zhen chags bzung 'dzin gyi mdud pa khrol cig/ phrag dog rung 
7b5(cha'o): sang zhig/ kye rigs kyi bu/ bka' lung gi dgongs pa ma len pas/ bla ma'i gdam ngagthugs dgos ma chod pas/ grub mtha' khas len ma chod dang / sgom nor sems la ma bu 
7b6(cha'o): ma 'phrod pa/ sgom pa spong par du ma gtong zhig/ dran can gyi bla ma dang ma bral zhig/ ces thugs kyi dkyil du zhig/ dad pas dag pa'i grogs/ ngan rtogs sems kyi gnya' 
8a1(cha'o): gnon/ brtson 'grus thar pa'i sgul ma/ bzang rtogs sems kyi cha bden/ dran rtog sems kyi tsho 'drul/ bya bar thar pa'i btan rkyen/ lta bsems kyi / 
8a2(cha'o): gnas gni/ sgom pa sems kyi gdar/ spyod pa sems kyi rtsal sbyangs/ nyon mongs sems kyi so lags/ de rnams la gdag pa zhus pa ma byed cig/ sgom pa nam mkha' 
8a3(cha'o): yongs khyab la/ mzshing dgongs pa mi 'dug ste/ log rtogs sprin gyi sgrib pa la/ sgom pa nyi zla 'dra ba btang / 'pho 'gyur dang re dgs g.yo 'gul la/ stong nyid sku mkhar 'dra ba 
8a4(cha'o): brten/ zhigs ral ba g.yo rtsol gyi dgra la/ bon nyid kyi dkor mdzod 'dra ba bstan/ sgrib pa dang bying rgod gza' la/ gsal la rtog pa med pa ston/ dbye dang zeo zog gi 'tshub

8b1(cha'o): rjen pa zhig/ nyon mongs rnam rtog gang byung yang / rang grol 'dzin med chen po zhig/ 'gag med rang shar rgya yan btang / rtsa bral rtsa mthong s ma zhig/ ma bcos spros bral 
8b2(cha'o): du btang / ci byas lhas med lhug par zhog/ phyogs med mtha' bral yul med du btang / nges med chal s hyid de zhog/ rang chas sku gsum lhun grub sgom/ bde gsal 'dzin 
8b3(cha'o): pa med pa mnyam par zhog/ brjod med bsam 'das sgra med sgom/ rang so ma bsud rzen par zhog/ thig med rang 'byung nyag gcig sgom/ ma spyod mie rtog la zhog/ dbyings nyid

8b5(cha'o): de ka'i ngag du btang / de yang sgom pa smra bsam brjod du med pa'o// kye ma kyi ma rigs kyi bu/ spyod pa ni sems nyid yid bzhin nor bu spyed/ rang rig ma bcos pa ni yid bzhin nor 
8b6(cha'o): bu yin/ spyod pa ni rang sems sangs rgyas kyi ngo bo spyod/ kun la khyab pa rang sems sangs rgyas yin/ spyad kyang su kyang thad pa mi 'dug ste/ kun gzhi byang chub sems sangs rgyas / 
9a1(cha'o): yin/ mthong ba med pa'ngo mtshar che/ skad cig ma bral mgyogs pa spyod/ yang spyod pa 'ngo mtshar che/ 'gyu byed dran pa sna tshigs/ 'di yang rtogs bral med pa spyod na // 
9a2(cha'o): ngo mtshar che/ snga pbyi med pa sna tshogs ci 'pros kyang / bde gsal stong pa'i na du spyod/ sdug bsngal sbyang tshad ci 'byung yang / rang grol shig shig btang / de la dngos po gzugs kha dag 
9a3(cha'o): gang yang ma grub/ ce re lta bas stong gnsal g.yeng ba/ rigs kyi bu rang grol rang gi 'debss spyid/ tshe 'di yi 'khrul snang spu tsam yin/ gdam ngagsten pa'i bla ma ni/ kun tu

9a5(cha'o): 'brul nang lta bu yin/ mched dang tham dral yang 'brul dang lta bu yen/ la las pa ma gnyen tsan zang zhor yul mkhar gzugs brnyan sna tshigs 'khrul pa cung byung yang /

9b1(cha'o): la thug pa med/ gzhi la ltas na skye med 'khor ba dnges sug yin/ sangs rgyas sems su zhes pa yin/ sangs rgyas dgongs pa dngos kyi zin pa yin/ byang chub sems kyi 'bras bu / 
9b2(cha'o): dmar thag chod pa yin/ sems la bltas nas gsal stong dngos med yin/ rtsal la bltas na shar stong dus mnyam yin/ phyi ru bltas na snang ba sna tshogs dngos med yin/ bar du

10b1(cha'o): gzhi mtha' 'das ngag du snyam byed thag pa zhig shig btang / nyams len snang stong dngos med 'di/ gzhi mtha' 'das ngang du blo sems thag pa shig shig btang / kyi ma kyi ma rigs kyi bu// 
10b2(cha'o): 'gro ba 'dren pa'i nyag thag yin/ mun pa sel ba'i sgrin me 'khor bsgrol ba'i gru gzings tha rdams 'byed pa'i lde mig/ dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i nor bu 'di/ sangs nye lam bgrod 
10b3(cha'o): pa yin/ thugs dgongs lta bazhi gzhi yin de/ skyed sdug bzangngan mni bsam dang / 'khor 'das gnyis ka'i dgag sgrub la/ 'phral du snang bsal le drig ge ba/ shes pa khal 
10b4(cha'o): le khyug gi kha/ rig pa bun ni lang nge ba/ rnam rtog sal le spyod de ba/ nyams len pol le lhod de ba/ sangs rgyas ngo bo 'di rang / dge ba spyi mthun la spyod mkhan med/ a tsaM 
10b5(cha'o): ma rig pas khyab bdal la phyogs 'dzin byed/ rang gsal shes pa dri med la dgag sgrub byed/ snang ba nges med kun btags la rtog 'dzin byed/ snang ba dang bka' lung la phyogs tshad 
10b6(cha'o): 'dzin byed/ kun gzhi ka dag 'khrul zhig 'dod par byed/ yeng med nyon mongs rang grol la bzang ngan byed/ snang ba dang bon sku la chags sdang byed/ sems can sangs rgyas la 
11a1(cha'o): gzhan du r ba byed/ lha ba gtad med mtha' bral la/ rtsol ba 'dzin pa byed/ dug lnga ye shes la sang len byed/ khyim thabs 'khor ba'i gds thag la chags / 
11a2(cha'o): zhen byed/ nyams len yengs med sgom med la bye brag byed/ sdig pa dgos khur yin yang yang mkhan med do// spyod tshul bya med lhug pa chad 'dzin byed/ gdam ngag chu rgyun 
11a3(cha'o): bdud rtsi 'thung mkhan med/ bsrung mtshams phyogs med rgya yan gza' gtad med/ bka' lung du ma ro gcig la don du bye brag pye/ gzhan phan la 'jug gegs byed/ sgrod med 
11a4(cha'o): lam thabs tshod la rim pa bye/ a tsa ma la a tsa ma snying ro rje/ rigs kyi bu/ don ni gnyis med gcig tu dril la nyams su long / gzhi la dbus yang med la mtha' yang 
11a5(cha'o): med/ de'i na la snang ba sna tshogs ci shar yang sems la zhog/ mthong ba bltas pa'i mthong ma thag tu grol/ nges zhes la gdang nas grol ba gda'/ rig pa'i byor ba rang shar rig pa'i
